					add_mio_funds_gain_factor = 0.25
				}
			}

				}

					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = bombardier2
						add_idea = bombardier3
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_country_flag = CAN_bombardier_upgraded_2
					if = {
						limit = { has_idea = canada_bombardier }
						swap_ideas = {
							remove_idea = bombardier2
							add_idea = bombardier3
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				effect_tooltip = {
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = canada_bombardier
						add_idea = bombardier2
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = CAN_cost_to_hire_tt
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_country_flag = CAN_bombardier_upgraded_1
					if = {
